### Primary Cause: Legacy-Migration Timeout

Yes, the hypothesis is basically correct, but too narrow.

It hangs here:

- Shell timeout fires at [legacy-migration.ts](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia-os/shell/src/lib/legacy-migration.ts:170):
```ts
result = await withTimeout(
  agentAuthLegacyMigrate(migrateOpts),
  MIGRATE_TIMEOUT_MS,
  `legacy-migration timeout after ${MIGRATE_TIMEOUT_MS}ms`,
);
```

- Agent handler is blocked here: [ipc-handlers.ts](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia-agent/packages/runtime/src/auth/ipc-hand
lers.ts:189)
```ts
await saveAuth(state);
```

- `saveAuth()` blocks at [auth-store.ts](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia-agent/packages/runtime/src/utils/auth-store.ts:257
):
```ts
const password = await ensureMasterPassword();
```

- First-time bootstrap then calls:
  - [auth-store.ts:167](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia-agent/packages/runtime/src/utils/auth-store.ts:167) `getMasterPassw
ord(...)`
  - [auth-store.ts:173](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia-agent/packages/runtime/src/utils/auth-store.ts:173) `setMasterPassw
ord(...)`

- Windows keyring uses synchronous PowerShell process spawning at [keyring.ts:299](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia-agent/pa
ckages/runtime/src/utils/keyring.ts:299):
```ts
return env.exec("powershell", [...], { timeoutMs: 10000 });
```

Bluntly: the agent is not dead. The handler is blocking the Node event loop inside `spawnSync("powershell", ...)`. Firs
t-time Windows bootstrap can do up to three expensive PowerShell + `Add-Type` runs: availability probe, `CredRead`, the
n `CredWrite`. The shell-side 5s timeout is too short and misdiagnoses a slow credential bootstrap as migration failure
.

Patch:

```diff
diff --git a/shell/src/lib/legacy-migration.ts b/shell/src/lib/legacy-migration.ts
@@
-const MIGRATE_TIMEOUT_MS = 5_000;
+const MIGRATE_TIMEOUT_MS = 45_000;
```

```diff
diff --git a/shell/src/lib/agent-ipc.ts b/shell/src/lib/agent-ipc.ts
@@
 export async function agentAuthLegacyMigrate(
   opts: AgentAuthLegacyMigrateOpts,
 ): Promise<AgentAuthLegacyMigrateResult> {
@@
   const resp = await requestAgent<Wire>({
     request,
     responseType: "auth_legacy_migrate_response",
     id,
+    timeoutMs: 45_000,
   });
```

### Secondary Cause: BGM Failed To Fetch

Partially confirmed, with one correction.

Confirmed:
- BGM dev path resolves to `projects/naia-os/agent/src/bgm-server-bin.ts`.
- `spawn_youtube_bgm_server()` derives `agent_dir` from that source script at [lib.rs:1297](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia
-os/shell/src-tauri/src/lib.rs:1297).
- Windows resolver only checks `agent_dir/node_modules/.pnpm/tsx@*/node_modules/tsx/dist/cli.mjs` at [windows.rs:106](/
D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia-os/shell/src-tauri/src/platform/windows.rs:106).
- If that fails, Rust falls back to `npx.cmd tsx ...` at [lib.rs:1315](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia-os/shell/src-tauri/s
rc/lib.rs:1315).

Correction:
- In this workspace, `projects/naia-os/agent/node_modules/.bin/tsx.CMD` is **not present**. I verified `Test-Path` fals
e.
- `tsx.CMD` exists under `shell/src-tauri/target/debug/agent/node_modules/.bin`, but that does not help the dev source 
path.

Patch the resolver anyway, because relying only on `.pnpm/tsx@*` is brittle:

```diff
diff --git a/shell/src-tauri/src/platform/windows.rs b/shell/src-tauri/src/platform/windows.rs
@@
 pub(crate) fn resolve_tsx_from_agent(agent_dir: &std::path::Path) -> Option<(String, String)> {
+    let direct = agent_dir
+        .join("node_modules")
+        .join("tsx")
+        .join("dist")
+        .join("cli.mjs");
+    if direct.exists() {
+        return Some(("node".to_string(), direct.to_string_lossy().to_string()));
+    }
+
     // Find tsx cli.mjs inside pnpm store (version-agnostic glob)
     let pnpm_dir = agent_dir.join("node_modules").join(".pnpm");
```

Also fix the actual install state:

```powershell
cd D:\alpha-adk\projects\naia-os\agent
pnpm install
```

### Tertiary: Portal Deep-Link Absent

Confirmed. This is portal-flow mismatch.

Agent generates login URL at [oauth-flow.ts:131](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia-agent/packages/runtime/src/utils/oauth-flo
w.ts:131):

```ts
params.set("state", state);
params.set("app", "naia-os");
params.set("platform", process.platform);
```

Portal only preserves desktop callback for already-authenticated users when `redirect=desktop` is present at [proxy.ts:
86](/D:/alpha-adk/projects/naia.nextain.io/src/proxy.ts:86):

```ts
const redirect = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get("redirect");
const target = redirect === "desktop"
  ? `/${urlLocale}/callback?source=...`
  : `/${urlLocale}/dashboard`;
```

So already-logged-in users go to dashboard. No `/callback`, no `naia://auth?...`, no `Deep link received`.

Patch both sides for compatibility:

```diff
diff --git a/packages/runtime/src/utils/oauth-flow.ts b/packages/runtime/src/utils/oauth-flow.ts
@@
 params.set("state", state);
 params.set("app", "naia-os");
+params.set("redirect", "desktop");
+params.set("source", "desktop");
 params.set("platform", process.platform);
```

```diff
diff --git a/src/proxy.ts b/src/proxy.ts
@@
     const redirect = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get("redirect");
     const source = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get("source");
-    const target = redirect === "desktop"
+    const app = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get("app");
+    const isDesktopAuth = redirect === "desktop" || app === "naia-os";
+    const target = isDesktopAuth
       ? `/${urlLocale}/callback?source=${source === "embedded" ? "embedded" : "desktop"}`
       : `/${urlLocale}/dashboard`;
```

### Fix Order

1. Raise `auth_legacy_migrate` timeout to 45s and pass it through `agent-ipc.ts`.
2. Fix portal already-logged-in redirect compatibility.
3. Run `pnpm install` in `projects/naia-os/agent`, then patch `resolve_tsx_from_agent()` to check direct `node_modules/
tsx/dist/cli.mjs`.
4. Longer-term: stop using synchronous PowerShell `spawnSync` for Windows keyring bootstrap, or collapse probe/read/wri
te into fewer process launches. Current code blocks the entire agent process during credential operations.
